et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	And if it is swollen in the belly or under the ribs, then you must cut through until the moisture comes out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if it is swollen above its feet, the treatment is light and the repositioning to the mouth of the bladder is easy.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a .i. drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it [the dislocation] is in the stomach or the thigh, you must straighten it by wrapping it with a cloth wrapped around your hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and cause the moisture that is there to correct;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure,	and if other limbs are dislocated, and the joint remains;
si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	place the ball of your hand inside the wound, and pull up to the mouth of the wound;
puis i boute .i. oncine ou ij., et le trai fuer;	Then put one or two iron rods, and pull it out.
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier,	if the mouth of the worm boil is constricted due to the hot poultice that has come, do not stir it.
ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	then you must administer moist and fatty things;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	And apply soothing plasters, and let them rest in warm softening agents.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the bone is on the side, and you can put it back in place, apply what was said in the previous section about setting a live bone.
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	And if you cannot set it, break it into pieces and take nothing from the second joint.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, apply what was said in the previous section about dressing wounds with lint that comes from a female donkey.
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	And if bleeding occurs (when performing cautery), it must be stopped with tight restraint, and other treatments should be applied.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	I saw a woman whose womb had killed an infant, then consulted another physician about it, and the other revived the infant.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, an abscess appeared in the buttock and swelled so much that it opened up and began to rot.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called for the treatment, and I thought about it for a long time, but could not stop the wound from bleeding.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I place strong plaster, and from it comes out a bone, and after some days another one.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I marveled greatly, because the stomach has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought that it was the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em miglior point;	I sought the wound, and extracted several bones until the woman improved;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	And a woman endures for long times like this, and suddenly a little swelling occurs at the base.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	And I have not recorded this chapter for any other reason than that when the master discovers an unusual thing, he knows what remedy to apply.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to bring the marriage back to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres; et a .ij. tornans as .ij. chiés des .ij. liiens.	Here comes the form of the screw press, with which one measures books; and at each turn, both heads of the two levers move.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	The horns (whatever they refer to) should be more delicate for the restriction, and made of ebony or boxwood.
et soit li bouche dou fust .i. doi de large, et li marge des arbres .i. doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	And the mouth of the pipe should be two fingers wide, and the edge of the tree stump one finger thick, and long and a half palm.
et enmi les .ij. liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	And within the two leagues (units of measurement) should be two joints of this same pipe, which are sealed on both ends, half a palm long or slightly more.
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les .ij. cornes.	And this two joints are inserted into the mouth of the mallet for opening when turning the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, resembling something more subtle and lighter, should be made of ebony or boxwood, in the likeness of pincers.
et ait as .ij. chiés .ij. ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et .ij. dois de large;	and it should have two heads and two pincers, as you see, of a palm's length, and two fingers' width.
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor .i. lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes,	and when you see opening the woman, use all the instruments; make her sit on one bed, with her legs apart and her feet hanging.
puis boute les .ij. ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	then insert the two pincers into the woman together, and hold the head of the instrument under her thighs.
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	Then work your hand with all the instruments, just like you have done with the tweezers equally, according to the quantity that you see to open the mouth of the wound, until the pig lets out what it wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances; et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	These instruments are all covered and multiplied according to their resemblance; and when the surgeons have prepared them, he works more quickly, and higher for humans due to their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Never despise the instrument that you have not prepared, because their necessity is not excusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the afterbirth is retained during childbirth, you must command the patient to retain her lochia, and then make her vomit with emetics, and hold your hands on her mouth and nose.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	If she jumps due to this, it is good.
Se ceu non, si prent .i. pot, et fai .i. pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If this does not happen, take one pot and make a pessary or plug with it, and put herbs that can open the mouth of the woman, such as rue, anise, chamomile, cascara sagrada, and centaury;
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu; puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris,	All these herbs, or some of them, should be cooked or boiled in water over fire; then place a cane or the mouth of the pot on one end, and the other end into the mouth of the patient.
et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris; puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	and hold the plaster until the vapors enter the patient's body; then make him vomit, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the patient jumps up quickly.   \n\nSi ung de ses membres est ostez, si com avons dit, se le pointe et fai grosse pele pour que il ne refreigne, et on met en la plaie ung cestui qu’il ne demurra pas; si li coupe la veine ou il demande, et aucune fois ne demeurez pas.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature,	And if it remains after this treatment and does not heal, instruct the woman to moisten her left hand in sesame oil or mustard plaster, and then apply it to nature.
et quiere la secondine; et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	Then you should second her; and when she has found it, grasp it and stretch it little by little straight out, so that the husband does not feel pain during extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie; si venra et se desaerdra.	But you must move it gently to the right and left, and then pull; it will come out and discharge.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the mouth of the morsus (a bite or wound) is stretched open, we have said the treatment of emptying, and fumigation of herbs;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	And if it (the treatment) does not include all that we have said, ensure you do not pull;
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	But it is necessary that the one at the mouth of the bite (morsus), you tie it to the woman's cuxie, then cleanse it with ointment four-formula;
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer; mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	If it [the dislocation] is put back and will come forth, but nevertheless, when it could do so, a bad smell comes to the stomach and head, and it injures the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu: aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	Therefore, fumigations suitable for this are necessary: no ancient has proven fumigation of dill and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The form of the instrument with which one fumigates the woman to retain the flowers and the afterbirth is as follows:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it is of glass-like appearance similar to a cane, and place the head subtle in its nature, and the broad shoulders above the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	And let the fumigation be over the coals, and the tinder until it is burnt out, then start another.
de percier lou fondement	of piercing the foundation   (This line does not have a complete sentence in Old French and is likely an incomplete or fragmentary text)
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born without the foundation pierced, but rather it has been stopped up with some subtle syrup;   (This line does not have a complete sentence in Old French and is likely an incomplete or fragmentary text)
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	Therefore, it is necessary for the baler to pierce that spot with its tip at the appropriate depth, and not to pierce it with an acute spatula, and be careful that it does not touch the ligament.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then put on a soft cloth moistened with wine and oil, then treat with ointment until it heals.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will burst open again, place a splint of wood and leave it for many hours, and remove it when the child is seen to go into the bedrooms.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme; si covient coper celui soudement: si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	And sometimes comes this sudden swelling of wound or abscess; it is necessary to cover the affected area: if it is a wound, as we have said, with the lard of pig.
de la fistule dou fondement	of the fistula from the foundation
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des .ij. parties,	Fistulas that come from below the foundation are nodulation, and growth that comes above the foundation and in the space between two parts,
si a une fistule ou plusors; et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe,	If it has a fistula or more than one; and when that node is old, it works, and yet moisture wakes up pus or thin boils,
et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans; et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	Sometimes these fistulas are persistent; and they are recognized by those who notice either discharge or windiness when the patient has discharge, and occasionally it leaps one way or another.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge; et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	And if it has fistulas that penetrate to the bladder and halfway up the penis; and they reach to the joint of the thigh and notch of the pelvis.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one recognizes a persistent fistula at its base, and not a non-persistent one:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and you should press your index finger or base on it, and insert a fine awl of iron or steel into the fistula where there is no twisting.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou .i. poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	and if it has a twist, then insert a fine splint of wood or horsehair until you feel the splint or hair at your finger:
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you don't feel it, and there is no purulent discharge, wind, or worms, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie; si te haste dou curer.	Know that it does not pierce at all; hasten to cure it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula extends up to the bladder or the passage for urine, if it discharges urine and cannot be healed by medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it pierces up to the knee joint, then is the tendon coming to the surface;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If there is no twisting and the pain is around it, then it is definitely broken and no medicine or healing balm will help.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	And in these Persian blisters there is no cure except for work, and the vain efforts of foolish physicians who interfere.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit,	In those that are not Persian nor old, for the hope of healing by iron, as I have experienced.
et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos; et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and the patient lies between your hands on his back; and raise the legs up to his thighs, and have his thighs inclined toward his belly.
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	Then insert a tent of reed or plank if there is curvature, as long as you know where the dislocation comes from.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice,	If the patient feels it around the foundation, then you must insert your index finger there.
se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet; et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	if it feels pierced then you must find out what is inside, whether flesh or bone, then you know that it is penetrated;
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	Do not work on it if it cannot be healed.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	One should know that it can be well healed for some, but this happens seldom;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the aid that one gives, it is that one heats the subtle cautery according to the width of the fistula, as mentioned before;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement; et faice ceu .ij. fois ou .iij., tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and push it all hot into the fistula until it comes out from the base; and do this 2 or 3 times, as long as you know that these charred pieces should be burned, which are like a bird feather;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	And then cure the wound with softened tent (or bandage) soaked in butter, until the pain subsides, then apply a healing salve of warm and soothing oil.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien. Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If it heals like that, it is good. But if it cannot heal otherwise,
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if it enters, but does not pierce to the depth of the wound, place a thick covering of oil or syrup between your hand and the tent, and you will see the abscess under the cover of the bed.
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	If the head of the fistula begins to emerge, push it immediately in front of the tent, and then apply the cautery afterwards, until it reaches the tip of the tent.
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra; puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	The tent will be delivered, and it will shrink; then take out those charred items that seem like a feather of a bird, leaving nothing behind.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the flesh is cut open by itself and there is no exit, cauterize it with fire or medicinal ointment.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble .ij. bones choses: c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	Fire cauterization has two good effects: the burning of these charred items and the stopping of bleeding and removal of moisture.
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	Then treat the wound of moistened tents filled with butter or chopped herbs until the flesh is cooked in the butter;
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	Treat the wound with hard dry charcoal and dry medicine.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it will heal and not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes out to the full depth of the foundation and is separated from the body, push your finger or a probe into it and inquire about it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre .ij. est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des .iii. manieres:	If you feel the temptation and there is the cloth or leather or skin between two (2), where it is almost to pierce, have no fear except for the way of faith and hope through the administration of one of the three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	or you cauterize it as we have said, or you press it until it is deep, or if it breaks open, you apply poultice and cure it as first.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not go too deep, cover the thing that holds the foundation, and let the pus come out by its own will.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	Then heal, as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	In case it becomes healthy, you remove that covering and clean it when it is cut away from the foundation, either by pulling or with some other instrument pointed.
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	Then clean that festering sore in the wound as much as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	Then study to heal the wound and to keep the fistula in the part away from the foundation; it will be easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus,	And sometimes fistulas occur in this manner: and it is when you bite the tent (?) into the fistula, and it is where it touches the foundation below the skin surface.
si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	Take a tent (?) pierced through in this shape:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	Then insert one thread twisted into two, and push the tent into the fistula to its full length (?) at the end of the thread.    --> Then insert one thread twisted together, and push the tent all the way into the fistula up to the end of the thread.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is perforated along the foundation inside, then draw out the thread of that one, so that you push your finger or foundation.
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les .ij. chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse .i. jor ou .ij.;	And draw the head with the thread, and join together the two shoulders together, and hold one to another, and leave it for one day or two;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	And keep it fixed until the threads bind these charms that are between them, and they close.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then heal the wound until it is healed and healthy.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not pierce, make it pierce in all ways that you can, if it is not too deep.   Car il est doulent et grant peril por li laisser ouvir et non percier.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	It is not advisable to cover the wound while it is still gaping, and then cure it, as we have said, until it is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The shape of the spurred thorn from which they make the fistula is very sharp at one end and then it splits.
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and not on the other side, because it should not be covered where it should not be covered, as you see here.
des emorroydes	hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc,	Emorydes (embouchures) are in two ways: they are inside the foundation, like a grain of resin, and there are small and large ones, and on the outside there is blood, immediately.
et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor,	and sometimes there is one or several of them, and they are displaced from the foundation and the head of the foundation; but those that are displaced have little moisture.
et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	and they may still have some aqueous citron or some blood, and have the color of the body.
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	And the cure for those who have it within the foundation, it is that you command the patient to stretch out for going into bedrooms, until the foundations heal, and the children appear.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	Then hasten, and hold it with pliers or hold it with your nail, then strike it at its roots;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a .i. drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if the snakes cannot be held by their moisture, then take it with a cloth or cotton, or with a piece of chamois leather;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	And bind them to your wrists, then strike them, and sprinkle hot powders on top in place of cautery.
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, puis les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	Or you can cauterize it as the chapter on cautery says, and then treat it with other remedies until it is healed.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	And if the foundation cannot come out, then fumigate the patient with biting and harsh clysters to clean the area where the foundation is located, so that it can come out openly.
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	The patient should not prepare himself, and if his veins are forced from their foundation, the cure is easy;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	and you take hold of them with your nail or tweezers, and strike them, then cure as we have said, until they are healthy, and fear the incision with iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren .i. fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les .ij. chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille,	The suture should be made in this manner: take one twisted thread, put it on a needle, then pull the thread above and pierce the needle from the other side, and turn the two ends of the thread under the needle.
et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse .i. por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and if it is wide; pull out the thread first, then the cord, and draw out the needle, and do the same with all the others, and leave one for draining excess blood;
puis met sus le fondement .i. drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	then place a damp linen cloth soaked in rose oil or wax on the foundation and place it there, and instruct the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then leave it until it stops bleeding, and when it has stopped, treat the wound with ointment and other remedies until it heals;
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	The drying of fires or foundations
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Often happens the drying of fires in the intestines, and by constriction of nature, and when the disease is old and medicine has no effect.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	You must scrape off the surface with a spatula or your nail so it does not get wet;   Ou cautere de fer comande au malaide qu’il s’estrengne les poiz euz, et espoze les en une corde lisser, et li fist chaussez autour des membres ou il est dolens.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	Then cure it until it heals as necessary;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	And if it cannot heal, then repeat the shaving stronger than before, until it heals and is scorched;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then cure it until it heals.
dou fremit	the trembling
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Fumigations are small infestations around the body, and move much forward;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And sometimes the fever strikes, and one feels it like death shivering, and it comes upon the whole body, more in the hands than elsewhere.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the cure is that you take a cane of an ostrich feather or a strong bird's feather and place it on the shivering, so that the circles around the shivering are warmed.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand along the entire cane so that you cover it all around the shivering, and immerse it in it, and warm the shivering from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you wish to do so, make it like a catapult of tar or iron in this form, and let it be subtle within and traverse above:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	Do not pierce, for fear of causing pain, and press gently; And if you wish to cauterize the trembling (of a wound), as is explained in the chapter on cauterization.
de la forme dou clistere	of the shape of the clyster (enema)
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet; et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	Sometimes they make an enema of silver or arsenic, or melted tar or honey; and sometimes they make small and large instruments according to the ones brought in.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Therefore, when treating children who are weak and suffering, they are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the cluster is both small and large; it should be placed over a wide area where the belly is tied in this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez; et ait a l’un des costez .ij. pertus, et en l’autre .i.;	and there should be an opening where the belly is tied, as you see, and the cheeks should be pierced within; and at one side have two holes, and in the other one.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus,	and the belly where medicine is placed from the bladder or parchment should be pierced all around with small holes.
et ait entre chescun pertus .i. doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus .i. fil fort de fil crut tort en .x. ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	and place between each wound, that is to say, a space must be left, then push into these wounds, fill them with strong thread, twist it tightly around ten or twelve times, and bind the belly as if it were a goat's pouch;
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize; et c’est li forme dou cercle:	and when the medicine is inside, tie it with a strong thread to the instrument in front, then apply the plaster (clister); this is the form of a circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	Let the medicine neither be too hot nor too cold, and anoint the head of the plaster with oil or egg yolk, or similar substance, then gently push it in;
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses .ij. mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit,	Then the ministers press the patient with both hands together until he is completely visible, then remove the plaster, and wash the patient's legs at the opening.
et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet; et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	If the medicine is to be applied, burn it as much as possible; and if it makes him sleep all night, it will be more effective aid.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you plaster him in case of intestinal disease and the medicine hastens to heal, continue to apply it until he is cured.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por .i. enfant;	And if the hemorrhoids or abscesses are deep, the plaster should be as delicate as for a child;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	And this is the form of the subtle suppository on which the skin is stretched:
des plaies	for wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We have already said in the division about the treatment of wounds; now I will tell you about the care of hands and medicines, according to the completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are various according to how they were made, and according to the places where the wounds were made, and because of what they were caused.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things by which wounds are caused are by the thrusting of a spear, cutting with a sword and knife, or by a lance, arrow or dart, or similar things;
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	or according to the places in the body, such as a wound that falls on the neck, or the head, or the chest, or the belly, or the liver, and similar limbs;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	And I shall tell you the treatment for each wound, and I will begin with wounds of the head, for the reminder will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans,	If the wound comes on or in the head, and the bone is not broken, beware if it is a result of an arrow or similar things, and the skin is completely torn open and the wound is large.
et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	and you doubt the rise of an abscess: if it becomes hot, make it drain as soon as possible from the head itself, even if a little blood comes out of the wound, or it drains against the part injured.
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	And the sick person evacuate (empties) of wine and heavy foods.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if he does not want to purge, let his food be reduced, and he should drink no wine, nor eat meat.
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	And place on the wound, when an abscess develops there, cotton soaked in rose oil or only in stypic wine.
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	And if there is no abscess, place [something] on the wound, if it is fresh with all its blood, and it is not moved by air or powder, I shall say a little more about that shortly.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the fire has moved it, place some antiseptics on it until it is healed.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	If the wound is large like a sword's size and the lips cannot be brought together by force, bring them together by stitching, as I shall explain in abdominal wounds.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope; puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir,	If the wound is exposed of the bone, gaping and does not hold but only a little, press it; then cure the wound with medicine, and restore hard flesh in place of skin.
et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	Instruct the patient to eat large meats, such as cooked heads and wheat, also pulses and similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find or suspect rotten flesh without touching the bone, press the pus out of it all, and pour vinegar over it, then heal.
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	And if there is an artery in the wound or vein, which cannot be stopped without cauterization, and it cannot be stopped by medicines, then tie the artery with a thread if you find it dislocated.
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	And if that does not help, cauterize (it).
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	And if these wounds are small and simple, the cure is easy: and it is that you put this powder which hardens as soon as the arrows have moved.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est: pren encens une partie; sanc de dragon .ij. parties; chalz vive .iij. parties, et le poudre subtilment,	And the way to make the powder is: take one part of incense; two parts of dragon's blood; four parts of live coal, and grind it finely,   \( \)
et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	And press the wound, and hold it shut, until it heals well and is joined with all its blood.
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	And then tie it up well, and let it heal by itself if it does not swell; because medicine is not applied until it has healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And sometimes they do this with only charcoal when there is no incense or the blood of a dragon, but the wound has not healed over yet.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	If the wound has healed over, do not put this powder in it.   \] Et lors en est on pris a la poille d'une oye aisnee, et il en faisoit une poille de son cors; et ains que il en fist, li ars ne avoit mueit la plaie, car le poi de l'aigne est sanc remediatif.   \] And then they take the pod from an egg that has been incubated, and make a powder of its shell; and before they do this, the wound has not yet healed, because the point of the needle is a healing medicine.
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	Place some digestible oil onions or barley flour made with water and honey over it until it boils.
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then heal it with other treatments until it heals.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if a bone fracture comes with the wound and it is small, extract it with subtle tweezers.
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	And I will tell you next about the fractures of the head (skull).
de la plaie dou col	of the wound of the neck
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If there is a wound in the neck and it is simple (uncomplicated), there is no difference between this and one in the head, but if the nerve of the neck or the artery is cut.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it is the nerve, there is no other remedy but to let it heal and not put any restraint, because it harms the nerves and causes them to retreat;
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	And do not place anything cold on the wound, for the substance of nerves is cold, and the continuation of them is with the brain, which is the highest member.
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	but let the medicine be warm, like boiled water with sweet oil added and boiled again in sweet water.
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	and other stones of similar nature, and always moistened.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, then wrap it with strips of linen until it is healed.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and swollen and full of pus, pierce it or lower it.
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	And if the arteries are cut, and blood flows out, stop it, tie it, and cauterize it if necessary.
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	And if the spine of the neck is cut or the windpipe, and the conduct is kept, so that the meat goes through.
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	sew the windpipe above the neck of the throat, but do not touch the throat, instead place it back according to its natural shape.
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	And then let it come back into place, and leave it for some days, then heal it with hot poultices until it is healed;
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	If the wound presses against the bone, squeeze it;
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	And if there are bone fragments, pull them all out as you can, and leave those that you cannot get at until the wound heals.
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	Straighten and align the joint.
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	If the wound is fresh, sprinkle the powder that I have mentioned.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there is bone in the wound and it has a fistula, treat it as I have said in its chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	Of the wound from a spear or knife
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If it is a wound from a spear or knife and the wound gushes with gas, then look carefully whether the wound bubbles: know then that the wound is fatal.
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	and if it is not deep and the wound is fresh with all its blood, do not put any powder on it at first hour or bind it for the blood that clots prematurely,
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	return to the heart, and cut off the patient;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	But apply attracting ointment, and leave it on for two times per day;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	and if you have no ointment, place soft cotton in the wound to draw out moisture.
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	and make the patient sleep on the wound for two days, or three, or more.
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	if no spasm, nor bad tremor of the heart, nor twinge of the entrails occurs.
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	And when you see good positions, know that the wound is healed.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Leave the cauteries and other treatments, as long as he is healthy;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	If it cannot heal, and opens again, know that there is a fistula; cure it as appropriate.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from a sword cut or knife, and it is simple (straight), whether deep or not, treat the part that is in front.
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	if it is large, to sew; and if it is small, to powder; and if it has penetrated into the bone, and there are pieces detached from it, treat the wound and pull out the fragments if they are protruding.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	and if they are not protruding, let the wound heal by itself, align the extraction.
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	And for other wounds on various limbs, the judgments are similar as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	the dislocation of the belly
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	The dislocation of the belly is great and medium-sized and small;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	when the large wound occurs once, the entrails or the intestinal nerves are penetrated;
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	And stitching is more difficult, and sometimes a small wound is worth more than a large one.
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	Because when repositioning the intestines, they should be inserted gradually rather than all at once.
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	because the intestines swell up quickly and become hard if inserted too forcefully.
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	and because the midline wound is more important, therefore move the intestines back to their place rather than with the other two.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	And know that the hernia of the belly is according to 4 types:
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	The two common hernias occur in the abdominal wall.
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	and the hernias of other parts of the body and two other specific hernias are common for other places;
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	And all these are more suitable with a stitching of the stomach, and I shall say one of them and declare it.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	When the wound is small, and nothing from the intestines protrudes,
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	And there are two ways to reattach it:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	For the smallness of the wound, as we have said,
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	For because the intestines are swollen due to the cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it is cold, heat it up in this manner:
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	Soak a sponge or one piece of linen cloth only in hot water,
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	And you cook in sharp squill and cyperus and spike,
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	and open the intestines until the inflammation is exposed;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	And sometimes this vinegar restraining is made, and it is boiled to disperse.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	And when you see swelling spreading out, if possible empty the intestines of water or air and ill-prepared or bad ones should be cooked,
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	for this way the entrance is closed to little thing;
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	and if it cannot enter, then make a small wound with an instrument for coping with hemorrhoids;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	and the first treatment is boiled that should be cut,
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	We should not cut it without great necessity nor have it.
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	and this is the instrument for splitting:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	if you make an incision within the hollow and do not spread it, observe its shape here:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	When the wound is expanded and the intestines burst forth,
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	If you reset it according to its natural form in its proper place,
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	if you have the power to do so, for this is necessary.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	When the wound is wide, and it is in the area below the belly,
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	you must make the patient lie down on his back,
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	And raise his legs higher than his head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	if it is in the part below the belly,
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	If the head and foot are lower than the parts below,
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	And similarly, if the rupture of the abdomen is in one of the two parts
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	if the broken part is higher than the other;
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	and thus one must treat as I say in large and small wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	for small wounds, use what is appropriate;
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	Then have a pious minister who anoints the entire wound with his hand,
et assemble les levres;	And press the lips;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	and this is the common way of stitching (or suturing);
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	and you take a needle or more, according to the size of the wound;
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	then leave one inch from the edge of the wound and sew with a needle and strong thread.
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	And pierce the two joints of the skin with the two sharp bones (or needles).
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	which is beneath the skin inside, as long as you make it penetrate from that part,
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	and join the two pieces of bone together.
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	Then tighten a double thread around the needle on each side,
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	Then assemble the two heads of the wound facing each other,
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	and leave one finger's width space, and insert another needle;
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	then tie the thread as you did with the first needle,
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and continue doing this according to what you need for the needles,
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	As long as the entire wound is held closed;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	and the needles be medium-sized, between thin and thick.
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	because thin needles pierce through the entire skin, and very thick ones cannot enter easily;
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	because they should be medium-sized.
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	And it is not advisable to push the needles too deep into the flesh and skin,
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	so as not to open the wound before the suture.
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	and then close the tips of the needles, so they do not prick the patient while sleeping,
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	and wrap silk or fabric around the tips of the needles to hold them in place.
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	And let it heal as the wound is healed;
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	and this method of stitching with needles is more suitable for small wounds.
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	because there is a needle or two there.
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second stitch is common
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	and that you join the two shoulder bones and the two shin bones together with a needle and thread of strong, medium thickness.
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz .iiij. ensamble,	and when you have pierced all four of them together,
si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	if you draw the needle back to the part where you began, in the manner of drawing draughts (= pulling the thread through the fabric)
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	And put space between each stitch the thickness of a small egg.
ceste costure sevent li home,	this stitching shall be for the man.
et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre,	and I sew a wound with one who had or stomach,
qui estoit navrez d’un coutel,	which had been wounded by a knife,
et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant,	And the wound was more than one palm wide,
et issoit des intestines bien .ij. palmes de grant,	and the intestines were two palm lengths wide,
et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	and the wound was in the abdomen.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit .xxiiij. houres fuer,	I brought back the intestines after it had been out for 24 hours,
et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a .xv. jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	And the wound was stitched for fifteen days, and healed, and became healthy.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And they had judged that he would die, and it was a miracle;
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en .i. leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	and did not care for ointment because I was in a place where there was none found, nor any medicine;
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel .ij. fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	and I put old cotton on the wound two times a day, and washed it with water of honey until it healed.
Or vos dirai les .ij. propres manieres de cousture:	And now I will tell you the two proper methods of sewing:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	Take the needle and thrust it from the outside part towards the inside up to that place.
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille,	when it has pierced the skin in a straight line, place the end of the thread or sewing where you have put the needle:
et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	and make it pierce from the inside part towards the outside up to that place.
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz,	And the understanding of this stitch is that you sew it like a weaver weaves fur.
et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	And leave the gap once from one side and return it from the other until the stitch is completely finished.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement,	The second method of stitching, which Galen specifically refers to as:
si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les .ij. parties ensamble naturelment,	is like someone who assembles the two parts naturally without using stitches:
et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	And apply one of the cheeks to the other cheek, in this manner:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement,	Stick an awl or the next cheek, and pierce only that spot,
et laisse les .ij. chiés dou syfac;	leave the two cheeks of the mirror.
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens,	then turn the awl and pierce it from the outer part to the inner one,
as .ij. chiés dou syfac;	2 heads of the shoulder
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en .ij. autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	then pierce one and the other in the outer part, up to that which is inside, in 2 heads of the mirror that are opposite each other on the same side.
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	and this is the most common way of stitching and healing.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent,	Galen said this word, and no one testifies against it.
c’on doit coudre le ventre a .ij. aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	One must sew the belly with two needles, where there is thread in each.
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	and one should insert one needle from one side, and the other from the other side, in the manner of those who sew sutures.
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre,	and know that when the hernia is within the belly,
si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	the stitching is more difficult than in other parts of the belly.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgement of the wound is similar to the judgements of other wounds:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee,	and it is that when you probe the fresh wound with all its blood, just as the surgeon has moved it,
si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout; puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char,	if you put back the intestines, and sew it up; then place powder reinforcing the flesh on top.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	And if the arm has moved it, place any ointment that is present upon it until the wound heals.
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	Cut the thread, and tie the stitches, and seal them with wax.
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then heal the wound as others, until it is healed.
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel,	if you do not have medicine, put cotton on it as soon as it starts to heal,
et le remue .ij. fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	And move it twice a day as long as it heals.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	For you do not need any other medicine in many cases when the wounds are simple;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz,	and if you doubt that the wound causes commonality with the main members,
si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset,	It is necessary that you soften linen lightly in warm oil or rose oil,
et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	and place it around the swellings, and under the sores.
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient,	and if there is pain or pus in the belly, and this happens repeatedly,
si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	If the laxatives made from black wine are weak, especially if the pus comes up to the intestines;
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	And pierce within, and know that when it is the large intestines, it is easier to heal than the small ones.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez,	The intestine called "yew" cannot heal when it is perforated,
et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	and it is because of the inflammation of the veins that are there, and because of the subtlety of the whole body, and the closeness of its nature to nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if the suture jumps out from the wound, replace it as with the intestine, while it is fresh;
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne,	And if it is old and turned or black, you must tie the black part where blood does not flow.
car il i a voinnes et arteres;	For there are veins and arteries.
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien,	Then cut what is between the ligament.
et met les .ij. chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	And hang the two heads (shoulders) below the part of the wound so that it aligns for the extraction when the blades fall and the wound bows.
de la routure dou boueil	of the boil rupture
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite,	When the intestines are torn, and the wound is small,
si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes,	If one can restore it in some men,
por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	because I have seen that a man was pierced or stabbed with a lance;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac,	and the wound was on the right side of the stomach,
et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	and it became swollen and turned into a fistula, and in it there were emissions and windiness;
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I treat it according to what I know, and I did not stop refining until it healed, and the wounds closed.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw the wounds heal, I feared that the patient had an illness in his belly;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	and he did not have any sickness, but improved with better nutrition and drinks.
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	and the experienced said that if there is a small wound in the intestines, it should be tied in this manner:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie,	Take large tweezers, then gather the lips of the wound.
et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les .ij. levres,	and when the tweezers have opened the mouth, put it on the two lips,
si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	when it extends its mouth above;
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier,	and then grip the head (of the patient) and hold it so that it cannot dislocate.
puis met .i. autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	then place another force after in that manner as before, until the wound is completely seized;
et cout la plaie.	then dress the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide,	If the head (of a part of the body) becomes swollen inside (the body), it brings no harm to the patient.
et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste,	and one can tie the intestine with a fine thread cut from the intestine of an animal.
en teil maniere:	in such a way:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez,	take the head (of the intestinal thread) and make it quite blunt.
et puis lie au chief de cest fil .i. fil de lin subtil tort,	And then tie this thread around the neck of it, that is to say, fine linen thread twisted.
puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	Then put the thread on a needle and sew the intestine, and remove it through the incision;
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	And this method of stitching up wounds is not stronger than by faith and hope.
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	If the wound is great and wide, especially if it is in one of the large intestines, there will be no help nor health, unless by subtlety.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	of a fistula or...
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule»,	All wounds or abscesses that heal are universally called "fistulas",
et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	and likewise when it is closed and healed.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor,	And a fistula, according to the truth, is a hard and white knot that does not cause pain,
et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	And it is as swollen as a feather of a bird;
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	sometimes it jumps clearly in a bow, and at other times it becomes thickened;
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	sometimes small, and at other times enough;
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char,	I have spoken about it in the section on wounds, that any wound that is not healed and there is no flesh;
ce n’est fuers que par une des .viiij. causes:	It is beyond doubt due to one of the 8 causes:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	this means, by an excess or deficiency of blood or humor:
ou por sa malice;	or because of a disease:
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	For because there is hard flesh within, under the lips, do not let it grow (hair).
ou il i a trop de bowe;	for there is too much phlegm.
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	when the loins are swollen and the matter is of bad quality.
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	for the medicine is not good in the treatment.
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	Because corruption is a form of pestilence;
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	because in the region the digestion is slow and health sluggish, and it tends to swell by nature;
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	there are veins or bones there;
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	and I have already shown all these causes, signs, and cures of medicine in the division.
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	Now I shall tell you the cure for a fistula made by handwork.
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	Know that fistulas occur in all members of the body;
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners,	because there are fistulas that come from large veins, arteries, and nerves,
ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes,	or in the intestines, bladder, kidneys, or any other part of the body.
ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	For the spine of the back, or for any joint of the hands or feet;
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	and if it affects the principal member property, and similar things.
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	And all the fistulas that are of this kind are of grave healing, and there is nothing but labor and ignorance to cure them.
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure,	And if there is any fistula that does not come up to the level I have said, and you have confidence in its cure,
et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	And you recognize it, take a tent of honey or iron, if its opening is straight, pierce it.
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc,	And if its opening is twisted, look for a fine tent of lead...
car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	because lead bends with the twisting.
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes,	and if its opening has been damaged and you cannot find it with tents,
si la clisterize par l’un des pertus,	If the incision is made through one of the wounds,
car la moistors si cort d’un pertus a autre, et la mundifie;	for moisture cuts from one wound to another, and it cleanses (it);
puis la quier saigement a ton pooir, que tu conoisses s’il i a os ou nerf, et est chevee em parfont,	then bind it with hemostatic power as you can, so that you know if there is bone or nerve, and it is completely closed,
et demande bien au malaide de la dolor qu’il sent au presser de ta main, et le leu ou il la sent;	and ask the patient carefully about the pain they feel when pressed by your hand, and the location where they feel it;
et quant tu savras vraiement le leu ou elle est, et s’elle est loing de jointure, ou de nerf, ou d’artere ou de voine,	And when you truly know where it is located, and if it is far from a joint, or a nerve, or an artery, or a vein,
ou en aucuns des leus que je t’ai dit, si la cope selonc ceu que je t’ai dit,	or in any of the locations that I have told you, if the arm is positioned according to what I have told you,
et oste fuer la fautreure et les chars corrumpues que sont dedens;	and cut out the false flesh and corrupt cartilage that are inside.
et puis la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee,	and then heal it when it is healed,
et se li fistule est bien parfonde de droit endroit, si covient que tu copes em parfont, tant com tu pues,	And if the fistula is properly penetrated straight through, it is necessary that you cut it all the way, as much as you can,
puis i met tentes moillies en medicine ague, et les boute jusc’au chief de la fistule,	then put wet bandages soaked in medicine on it, and push them up to the head of the fistula.
tant que li medicine corrode la superfluiteit qui est demoree au fons;	until the medicine dissolves the superfluidity that remains at the bottom;
et puis i met oignemens enjanrans sainne char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then put warm ointments on the healthy flesh, until it heals;
et s’il n’est sanez par ceu, si le cauterize si com nos avons dit,	And if it is not healthy by this [method], cauterize it as we have said,
et se li os est corrompus de la fistule, si le cope.	And if the bone is rotten from the wound, break it.
Se voinne ou ners ne te greve ou membres principelz, si com nos avons dit;	If a vein or nerve does not obstruct or affect the main limbs, as we have said;
et se li os est descovers, et il i a corruption et noiror, si lou reis tant que li corruption soit toute ostee,	And if the bone is exposed, and there is decay and blackness, cut it off while the decay is completely removed,
puis le cure de choses enjanrans char tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then heal the things that are harmful to the bone while it is healthy.
et s’il n’est sanez, et rent bowe si com devant,	and if it is not healthy, then bind it as before,
saiches que tu n’es mie alez jusc’a font:	know that you are not going as far as the fountainhead:
si descuevre et quier tant que tu soies au fons,	If you uncover [something] and want to go as deep as possible,
et oste toute la corruption, puis restore le leu;	and remove all the corruption, then reset the joint.
et s’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	and if it is thus healed, that is good.
Se ceu non, saiches que la corruption est trop en parfont, que tu n’i pues avenir;	But if not, know that the corruption is too deep that you can't reach it.
si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier a nature;	If there is no other remedy than natural rest.
et s’il i a i petit os corrumput, et tu le pues traire as tenailles,	and if there is a little bone corrupted, and you can draw it with pliers,
si l’estrai a .i. estrument covenauble a ceu,	if it is drawn out with one instrument convenient for this.
et s’il i a maint os, si les trai trestoz, ne n’en laissier nes un;	and if there are several bones, draw them all out, do not leave any of them.
et se li moistor te fait contraire, et il n’i a error ne paour,	And if moisture opposes you, and there is no mistake or fear,
si cope et moistor et char, et delivre les os.	If flesh and moisture bind the bones together, then release the bones.
Et se tu ne les pues oster a une houre, si met sus la plaie chose enjanrant porriture,	And if you cannot remove them within an hour, place something irritating purgative on the wound,
et laisse tant que li leus soit porris entor les os,	And let the muscles be swollen around the bones,
et adonc si avront plus legierement les os;	And then they will have more easily moveable bones;
et se c’est uns grans os, si com de jambe ou de cuisse,	and if it is a large bone such as the thigh or the leg,
si reis tant soulement la corruption tant que li noiror soit toute ostee,	if you press only the corruption until all the blackness disappears,
puis restoure la plaie;	Then restore the wound;
et s’il en i a grant partie dou corrumput, et vient jusc’a mole de l’os;	And if there is much rotten part in it, reaching down to the bone.
si le covient soier et coper tout jusc’a la corruption, et puis le cure tant qu’il soit soudez;	it must be cut and covered up to the corruption, and then let it heal until it is healed.
et je te dirai d’une fistule qui avint .i. home en sa jambe,	And I will tell you about a fistula that happened to one man in his leg,
si que tu i preignes exemple et aide en ton ovraige.	If you take an example and help in your work.
Il fut .i. jovencelz entor .xxx. ans, qui ot une dolor en sa jambe d’une cause que vint dedens le cors,	There was a young man around thirty years old who had pain in his leg due to a cause that came from within the body.
tant que les matieres vinrent a la jambe, et fut enflee d’un gros aposteme, et n’ot point de cause defuer por ovrir;	The matters kept coming to the leg and a large abscess erupted, and there was no other reason for it to open.
mais li mire par lor folie ovrerent tant sus que li apostemes ovri,	but the fools opened them too much so that the abscesses burst open,
